# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

Use `sg_list_repos` to discover available repositories before searching.


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

I've identified **21 primary Go source files** that implement plugin signature verification across three main areas:

### 1. **Core Signature Management** (3 files)
- **manifest.go** - Reads, parses, and verifies plugin MANIFEST.txt files with PGP signatures and SHA256 hash verification
- **signature.go** - Validates signature status (valid/invalid/modified/unsigned)
- **authorizer.go** - Enforces the unsigned plugin allowlist with `CanLoadPlugin()` method

### 2. **Key Retrieval** (3 files)
- **statickey/static_retriever.go** - Hardcoded Grafana Labs public key
- **keyretriever/retriever.go** - Service provider for key retrieval
- **dynamic/dynamic_retriever.go** - Fetches and caches keys from Grafana.com API

### 3. **Plugin Loading Pipeline** (5 files)
- **bootstrap/steps.go** - Calculates signature during plugin construction
- **validation/steps.go** - Validates signatures during plugin loading
- **pipeline/steps.go** - Integration of validation into the pipeline
- Configuration and wire setup files

### 4. **Configuration & Models** (5+ files)
- Plugin models with SignatureStatus and SignatureType enums
- Configuration loading from `allow_loading_unsigned_plugins` setting
- Plugin interfaces and dependency injection setup

The complete analysis with 35 key symbols and a detailed execution chain has been saved to `/workspace/answer.json`.

The `Validation` struct implements the `Validator` interface with:\\n\\n- `ValidateSignature()`: Main validation method that checks signature status and handles inheritance for nested plugins\\n  - Returns success for valid signatures\\n  - Returns success for core/internal plugins\\n  - Returns success for inherited valid signatures from parent plugins\\n  - Calls `CanLoadPlugin()` for unsigned plugins to check the allowlist\\n  - Returns errors for invalid and modified signatures\\n\\n## Unsigned Plugin Allowlist Enforcement\\n\\nThe allowlist enforcement is implemented in `pkg/plugins/manager/signature/authorizer.go`. The `UnsignedPluginAuthorizer` struct provides:\\n\\n- `CanLoadPlugin()`: Authorizes plugin loading by:\\n  - Allowing all non-unsigned plugins\\n  - Allowing unsigned plugins in dev mode\\n  - Checking if the plugin ID is in the `PluginsAllowUnsigned` configuration list\\n  - Denying unsigned plugins not in the allowlist\\n\\n- `ProvideOSSAuthorizer()`: Factory function creating the authorizer from `PluginManagementCfg`\\n\\nThe allowlist configuration is loaded in `pkg/setting/setting_plugins.go` from the `[plugins]` section's `allow_loading_unsigned_plugins` setting, which accepts a comma-separated list of plugin IDs. The list is stored in `pkg/plugins/config/config.go` as `PluginsAllowUnsigned` in `PluginManagementCfg`.\\n\\n## Key Management\\n\\nPublic key retrieval for signature verification is handled through a two-tier system:\\n\\n1. **Static Keys** (`pkg/plugins/manager/signature/statickey/static_retriever.go`): Contains a hardcoded Grafana Labs public key used as fallback\\n2. **Dynamic Keys** (`pkg/services/pluginsintegration/keyretriever/dynamic/dynamic_retriever.go`): Downloads and caches keys from the Grafana.com API, updating every 10 days\\n\\nThe key retriever service (`pkg/services/pluginsintegration/keyretriever/retriever.go`) acts as a facade, selecting between dynamic and static retrieval based on configuration.\\n\\n## Plugin Loading Pipeline\\n\\nSignature calculation and validation are integrated into the plugin loading pipeline:\\n\\n1. **Bootstrap Stage** (`pkg/plugins/manager/pipeline/bootstrap/steps.go`): `DefaultConstructor.Construct()` calls `SignatureValidationStep()` creates a validation function that calls `Validation.ValidateSignature()` for each plugin\\n\\n3. **Configuration Integration** (`pkg/plugins/config/config.go`): `PluginManagementCfg` passes the allowlist to the `UnsignedPluginAuthorizer`\\n\\n## Models and Interfaces\\n\\nKey types are defined in `pkg/plugins/models.go`:\\n- `SignatureStatus`: \\\"internal\\\", \\\"valid\\\", \\\"invalid\\\", \\\"modified\\\", \\\"unsigned\\\"\\n- `SignatureType`: \\\"grafana\\\", \\\"commercial\\\", \\\"community\\\", \\\"private\\\", \\\"private-glob\\\"\\n\\nCore interfaces in `pkg/plugins/ifaces.go`:\\n- `PluginLoaderAuthorizer`: Authorizes plugin loading\\n- `SignatureCalculator`: Calculates plugin signature state\\n- `KeyRetriever`: Retrieves public keys for verification\\n- `KeyStore`: Stores cached public keys\\n\\n## API and Settings\\n\\nThe plugin API (`pkg/api/plugins.go`) and frontend settings (`pkg/api/frontendsettings.go`) expose plugin signature information. The `Validation` struct implements the `Validator` interface with:\\n\\n- `ValidateSignature()`: Main validation method that checks signature status and handles inheritance for nested plugins\\n  - Returns success for valid signatures\\n  - Returns success for core/internal plugins\\n  - Returns success for inherited valid signatures from parent plugins\\n  - Calls `CanLoadPlugin()` for unsigned plugins to check the allowlist\\n  - Returns errors for invalid and modified signatures\\n\\n## Unsigned Plugin Allowlist Enforcement\\n\\nThe allowlist enforcement is implemented in `pkg/plugins/manager/signature/authorizer.go`. The `UnsignedPluginAuthorizer` struct provides:\\n\\n- `CanLoadPlugin()`: Authorizes plugin loading by:\\n  - Allowing all non-unsigned plugins\\n  - Allowing unsigned plugins in dev mode\\n  - Checking if the plugin ID is in the `PluginsAllowUnsigned` configuration list\\n  - Denying unsigned plugins not in the allowlist\\n\\n- `ProvideOSSAuthorizer()`: Factory function creating the authorizer from `PluginManagementCfg`\\n\\nThe allowlist configuration is loaded in `pkg/setting/setting_plugins.go` from the `[plugins]` section's `allow_loading_unsigned_plugins` setting, which accepts a comma-separated list of plugin IDs. The list is stored in `pkg/plugins/config/config.go` as `PluginsAllowUnsigned` in `PluginManagementCfg`.\\n\\n## Key Management\\n\\nPublic key retrieval for signature verification is handled through a two-tier system:\\n\\n1. **Static Keys** (`pkg/plugins/manager/signature/statickey/static_retriever.go`): Contains a hardcoded Grafana Labs public key used as fallback\\n2. **Dynamic Keys** (`pkg/services/pluginsintegration/keyretriever/dynamic/dynamic_retriever.go`): Downloads and caches keys from the Grafana.com API, updating every 10 days\\n\\nThe key retriever service (`pkg/services/pluginsintegration/keyretriever/retriever.go`) acts as a facade, selecting between dynamic and static retrieval based on configuration.\\n\\n## Plugin Loading Pipeline\\n\\nSignature calculation and validation are integrated into the plugin loading pipeline:\\n\\n1. **Bootstrap Stage** (`pkg/plugins/manager/pipeline/bootstrap/steps.go`): `DefaultConstructor.Construct()` calls `SignatureCalculator.Calculate()` to determine the plugin's signature status before creating the plugin object\\n\\n2. **Validation Stage** (`pkg/services/pluginsintegration/pipeline/steps.go`): `SignatureValidationStep()` creates a validation function that calls `Validation.ValidateSignature()` for each plugin\\n\\n3. **Configuration Integration** (`pkg/plugins/config/config.go`): `PluginManagementCfg` passes the allowlist to the `UnsignedPluginAuthorizer`\\n\\n## Models and Interfaces\\n\\nKey types are defined in `pkg/plugins/models.go`:\\n- `SignatureStatus`: \\\"internal\\\", \\\"valid\\\", \\\"invalid\\\", \\\"modified\\\", \\\"unsigned\\\"\\n- `SignatureType`: \\\"grafana\\\", \\\"commercial\\\", \\\"community\\\", \\\"private\\\", \\\"private-glob\\\"\\n\\nCore interfaces in `pkg/plugins/ifaces.go`:\\n- `PluginLoaderAuthorizer`: Authorizes plugin loading\\n- `SignatureCalculator`: Calculates plugin signature state\\n- `KeyRetriever`: Retrieves public keys for verification\\n- `KeyStore`: Stores cached public keys\\n\\n## API and Settings\\n\\nThe plugin API (`pkg/api/plugins.go`) and frontend settings (`pkg/api/frontendsettings.go`) expose plugin signature information. Wire dependency injection setup is configured in `pkg/services/pluginsintegration/pluginsintegration.go` and auto-generated in `pkg/server/wire_gen.go`.\"\n}\n",
